<DESCRIPTION>ANNUAL PERFORMANCE INCENTIVE PLAN FOR EXECUTIVE OFFICERS
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Annual Performance Incentive Plan for Executive Officers</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 10.19 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="ARIAL"
SIZE="2"><B>Microsoft Corporation </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>Annual Performance Bonus Plan </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"
ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>for Executive Officers </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">(Effective July&nbsp;1, 2007) </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>1. Purpose of the Plan </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">This Microsoft
Corporation Annual Performance Bonus Plan for Executive Officers (the &#147;Plan&#148;) is designed to motivate Plan participants to achieve the financial and other objectives of Microsoft Corporation (&#147;Microsoft&#148;). </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>2. Eligibility and Participation </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL"
SIZE="2">Executive officers of Microsoft (&#147;Executive Officers&#148;), including the Chief Executive Officer (&#147;CEO&#148;), are automatically eligible to participate in the Plan and, therefore, are each referred to herein as a
&#147;Participant.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>3. Administration </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">The Microsoft Corporation Compensation Committee (&#147;Compensation Committee&#148;) administers the Plan. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>4.
Establishment of Performance-Based Commitments </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">The CEO in consultation with Microsoft&#146;s Board of Directors
(&#147;Board&#148;) shall establish annually his performance-based commitments (the &#147;Commitments&#148;) for each fiscal year (the &#147;Performance Year&#148;). For all other Participants, the CEO shall approve the Participant&#146;s
Commitments for each Performance Year. The Commitments may be based on organizational and/or individual goals, and may include quantitative and/or qualitative goals. Commitments may be based on the Executive&#146;s responsibilities and may include
financial or strategic measures, including: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">revenue, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">operations excellence, and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">efficiency and productivity. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>5. Determination of
Bonus Amounts </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><U>Approval of CEO Bonus</U>. The independent members of the Board determine the CEO&#146;s </FONT>
</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify">
<FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">bonus after receiving a recommendation from the Compensation Committee. The Compensation Committee makes its recommendation after considering the results of the CEO
performance review conducted by the Microsoft Corporation Governance and Nominating Committee. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><U>Approval of Other Executive
Officer Bonuses</U>. The Compensation Committee of the Board determines the bonuses of Participants other than the CEO after receiving a recommendation from the CEO. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"
ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><U>Basis of Bonus Recommendations</U>. Bonus recommendations will be based on an assessment of the extent to which each Participant achieved his Commitments and other feedback and input from the Senior
Vice President, Human Resources. The following factors may be considered in assessing achievement of Commitments: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">difficulty of the Commitments, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">business environment in which the Commitments were achieved; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">consistency and reliability of performance across Commitments and throughout the Performance Year, </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">the Participant&#146;s going above and beyond commitments and expectations, and </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="justify"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">the Participant&#146;s degree of excellence </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL"
SIZE="2">Bonus recommendations will be determined as a percentage of a Participant&#146;s bonus eligible salary. The Compensation Committee will establish potential bonus ranges based on Participants&#146; roles. The maximum potential bonus that
will apply to any Participant is 200% of bonus eligible salary. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><U>Bonus Eligible Salary</U>. Bonus eligible salary is a
Participant&#146;s base salary calculated from eligible payroll earnings during the Performance Year while the employee is in active status as an Executive Officer. If a Participant is hired after March&nbsp;31 of a Performance Year, and thus, is
ineligible for a bonus for such Performance Year, bonus eligible salary for the following Performance Year shall include base salary during the period commencing on the Participant&#146;s date of hire, and ending on the last day of such Performance
Year. Bonus eligible salary shall exclude any base salary accounted for under any other bonus plan or program sponsored by Microsoft. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL"
SIZE="2"><U>Employment Requirement</U>. For each Performance Year, no bonus will be paid unless the Participant is employed by Microsoft prior to March&nbsp;31 of the Performance Year and remains employed by Microsoft through the last day of such
Performance Year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>7. Payment of Bonuses </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT
FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">Bonuses shall be paid in cash as soon as practicable following the end of a Performance Year, but in no event later than September&nbsp;30 following the conclusion of the Performance Year. Bonus payments shall be reduced for
taxes and other legally required withholdings. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>8. Interpretation, Amendment and Termination of the Plan </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">The Compensation Committee has the discretionary authority to: construe and interpret the terms of the Plan; to determine, in accordance with the
provisions of the Plan, the existence or non-existence, nature and amount of the rights and benefits of all persons under the Plan; and to amend or terminate the Plan at any time; provided that all such authority shall be limited to the extent
required to comply with applicable law outside the United States. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>9. Employment at Will (U.S. Employees Only) </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">Neither this Plan nor any action or communication under this Plan: (1)&nbsp;gives any employee any right with respect to employment or continuation
of current employment with Microsoft or its subsidiaries or </FONT>
</P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify">
<FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">to employment that is not terminable at will, or (2)&nbsp;makes any employee&#146;s employment with Microsoft or its subsidiaries for any minimum or fixed period.
Employment by Microsoft (or the Microsoft subsidiary that is the employer) may be terminated by either the employee or the employer at any time, for any reason or no reason, with or without cause, and with or without notice or any kind of pre- or
post-termination warning, discipline or procedure. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2"><B>10. General Provisions </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">A. <U>Rights Unsecured</U>. The right of a Participant or his or her beneficiary to receive a bonus under the Plan shall be an unsecured claim
against the general assets of Microsoft. The Plan at all times shall be considered entirely unfunded for tax purposes. Microsoft&#146;s obligation under this Plan shall be that of an unfunded and unsecured promise to pay money in the future.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">B. <U>Nonalienation of Benefits</U>. Bonuses are not subject in any manner to anticipation, alienation, sale, transfer, assignment,
pledge, encumbrance, charge, garnishment, execution or levy of any kind, either voluntary or involuntary, and any attempt to anticipate, alienate, sell, transfer, assign, pledge, encumber, charge or otherwise dispose of any right to any benefits
payable hereunder, will be null and void and not binding on Microsoft. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">C. <U>Severability</U>. If any provision of the Plan shall be
held invalid or illegal for any reason, any illegality or invalidity shall not affect the remaining parts of the Plan, but the Plan shall be construed and enforced as if the illegal or invalid provision had never been inserted. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%" ALIGN="justify"><FONT FACE="ARIAL" SIZE="2">D. <U>Applicable Law and Venue</U>. To the extent not preempted by federal law, the Plan shall be governed by the laws of the State of Washington.
If Microsoft or any Participant (or beneficiary) initiates litigation related to this Plan, the venue for such action will be in King County, Washington. </FONT></P>
</BODY></HTML>
</TEXT>
